<p style="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.2pt"><b>Item 5.07&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239;&#8239; Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</b></p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.2pt">On June 11, 2025, Caterpillar Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;)
held a virtual 2025 Annual Shareholders Meeting (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). Set forth below are the voting results for each of
the matters submitted to a vote of the Company&#8217;s shareholders at the Annual Meeting.</p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.2pt"><b>Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure</b></p>

<p style="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 4.55pt 0pt 5.2pt">On
June 11, 2025, the Board of Directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of one dollar and fifty-one cents ($1.51) per share of Company
common stock, payable on August 20, 2025 to shareholders of record at the close of business on July 21, 2025. The per share dividend of
$1.51 is an increase of ten cents from the previous quarterly dividend of $1.41 per share. On the same date, the Company issued a press
release announcing the dividend increase, a copy of which is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1.</p>

<p style="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 5.2pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 271pt 0pt 0">Global Government &amp; Corporate Affairs 832-573-0958 Tiffany.Heikkila@cat.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><B><U>Caterpillar Inc. Increases
Dividend</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3pt 0pt 0">IRVING, Texas, June 11, 2025 &ndash; The Board of Directors
of Caterpillar Inc. (NYSE: CAT) voted today to raise the quarterly dividend by 10 cents, a seven percent increase, to one dollar and
fifty-one cents ($1.51) per share of common stock, payable Aug. 20 to shareholders of record at close of business July 21. Caterpillar
expects to continue to return substantially all Machinery, Energy &amp; Transportation (ME&amp;T) free cash flow to shareholders over
time through dividends and share repurchases.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;Continued delivery on our enterprise strategy for long-term
profitable growth, combined with strong operating performance, has led to robust ME&amp;T free cash flow,&rdquo; said Caterpillar CEO
Joe Creed. &ldquo;We are pleased to increase our quarterly dividend and retain our continued presence on the S&amp;P 500 Dividend Aristocrats
Index.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 3pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">Caterpillar has paid a cash
dividend every year since the company was formed and has paid a quarterly dividend since 1933. Caterpillar has paid higher annual dividends
to shareholders for 31 consecutive years and is recognized as a member of the S&amp;P 500 Dividend Aristocrats Index.</FONT>&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt"><B>About Caterpillar</B>&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10.5pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 2pt 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">With 2024 sales and revenues
of $64.8 billion, Caterpillar Inc. is the world&rsquo;s leading manufacturer of construction and mining equipment, off-highway diesel
and natural gas engines, industrial gas turbines and diesel-electric locomotives. For 100 years, we&rsquo;ve been helping</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt">(more)</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 9pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&#160;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 9pt"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">-<!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence -->-</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 12pt">customers build a better, more sustainable
world and are committed and contributing to a reduced-carbon future. Our innovative products and services, backed by our global dealer
network, provide exceptional value that helps customers succeed. Caterpillar does business on every continent, principally operating
through three primary segments &ndash; Construction Industries, Resource Industries and Energy &amp; Transportation &ndash; and providing
financing and related services through our Financial Products segment. Visit us at caterpillar.com or join the conversation on our social
media channels at caterpillar.com/en/news/social-media.html.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>
